v500
Waterfall Jump
Jump from the waterfall 3 times and get
more than 500m total distance to clear.
Target Jump
Head toward the numbered boards and jump.
Try to break'm all. You can miss up to 3.
Balloon Attack
Head towards the moving balloons and jump.
Try to bust at least 7 of them.
Bunny Hop
Bunny hop and reach the goal within the
time limit. You can miss up to 5 times.
Submarine
Submarine through tunnels in the
allotted time. You can miss 5 times.
Loop
Do 10 loops in the allotted amount
of time.
Barrel Roll
Do 10 barrel rolls in the allotted
amount of time.

from 1 to 15 within the time limit.
v5000
Beach Balloon Run
Pass through numbered score gates
and try to get 5000 points.
1)You need to increase speed to jump far.
2)Squeeze the trigger hard to get a good
  jump start at the line.
3)To dash from a standstill, push UP and
  quickly squeeze the accelerator.
1)In order to land where you want, it's
  important to line yourself up before
  you hit the jump.
2)Adjust your steering and acceleration
  when you jump.
1)Watch the balloon patterns. Use your
  dash and techniques optimally.
2)Timing is everything here.
1)The Bunny Hop: a trick performed by using
  your feet and the waves to get air.
2)Release the accelerator and quickly press
  DOWN.
3)Learn to adjust your timing to get the
  best handling.
Submerging after jumping is called 
a "Submarine". Hold UP on your controller
right after jumping.
Forward/backward spins after 
jumping are called "Loops".
Press UP and DOWN right after jumping.
You can't loop unless you jump high.
Left/right spins after jumping are
called "Barrel Rolls".
Press LEFT and RIGHT right after jumping.
You can't spin unless you jump high.
1)Use the jumps and the bunny hop technique
  to go through the gates on the course.
2)Try to memorize the positions of the
  numbered gates on the course.
3)Release trigger + push DOWN to bunny hop.
1)Try to estimate the beach ball's
  direction and adjust your control.
2)Be careful, once you pass by a gate you
  can no longer earn a score from it.
